     <div class="post">
      <h1 class="postTitle">
       The 150 Best Online Flash Games
      </h1>
      <div class="postMetaSingle">
       by Daniel Scocco on Monday, October 6th, 2008
      </div>
      <script type="text/javascript">
       &lt;!--
ch_client = "gadgets";
ch_type = "mpu";
ch_width = 468;

ch_color_title = "3c65a4";

      <script src="http://scripts.chitika.net/eminimalls/amm.js" type="text/javascript">
      </script>
      <div class="postContent">
       <p>
        It was a long and exhausting task: playing hundreds of online games for hours in a row, day after day. It was hard, but someone had to do it.
       </p>
       <p>
        The result is the list that you will find below. Enjoy!
       </p>
       <h2>
        Action Games
       </h2>
       <p>
        <strong>
         1. IndestructoTank
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="indestructotank game" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/indestructotankgame.jpg" title="indestructotankgame" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        As you probably guessed, on this game, you get to drive an indestructible tank around. Once attacked by enemies bombs, the tank will be blasted into the sky and you will be able to hit the helicopters and planes. The more enemies you manage to take down on a single combo, the more points you earn. Make sure to reach the required experience points before your fuel ends.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.newgrounds.com/portal/view/371290" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play IndestructoTank
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         2. Electricman2HS
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="electricman2hs flash" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/electricman2hsflash.jpg" title="electricman2hs flash" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        A fighting game where you need to beat down several opponents at the same time. The variety of kicks, punches, throws and defensive movements really creates a funny experience. You even have slow motion movements a la Matrix!
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.kongregate.com/games/FreeWorldGroup/electricman2hs">
         <br/>
         Click here to play Electricman2HS
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         3. The Fancy Pants Adventure
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/fancypantsadventure.jpg" title="fancypantsadventure" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Think about
        <i>
         Sonic the Hedgehog
        </i>
        with a more clean design and some physics effects added. Ah, and a character that wears some really fancy pants! Just run through the levels, avoiding the monsters and collecting the swirls and trophies.
        <br/>
        <a href="http://www.kodiefiles.nl/games/hedgehog.swf">
         <br/>
         Click here to play The Fancy Pants Adventure
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         4. Dino Run
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/dinorun.jpg" title="dinorun" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        On this game you play a small dinosaur that is trying to escape the imminent extinction from a fallen meteor. You basically need to run among obstacles, hills and fellow dinosaurs that are also trying to escape. Putting it short: Run like there is no tomorrow!
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.pixeljam.com/dinorun/" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Dino Run
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         5. Matrix Rampage
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="matrix rampage" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/matrixrampage.jpg" title="matrixrampage" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        The Matrix fans out there will have fun with this one. You play as Neo in this game, jumping to and from floors on buildings and killing agents along the way. Guns, swords, staffs and pretty much everything else on the scenario can be used to get the job done.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://matrix-rampage.freeonlinegames.com/" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Matrix Rampage
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         6. Amorphous+
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="amorphous" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/amorphous.jpg" title="amorphous" width="399"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        The Gooples are all around you. They are colored bubbles that float around trying to kill you. Luckily, you are not alone. You have a huge-ass knife to cleave them all!
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.kongregate.com/games/innocuousGames/amorphous" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Amorphous+
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         7. Double Wires
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="double wires game" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/doublewiresgames.jpg" title="double wires game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Ever wanted to fly around like Spider Man? With this little Flash game, you can get close to it. Youll use your mouse to shoot two wires and prevent the little guy from falling. The objective is to go as far as possible.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.freewebarcade.com/game/double-wires/" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Double Wires
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         8. Final Ninja
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="final ninja" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/finalninja.jpg" title="final ninja" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        We couldnt leave ninja games out of the list, right? On Final Ninja, you command a little (but badass) ninja on a side-scrolling adventure. Your tool belt comes with throwing stars, a grappling rope and the ability to become invisible. Pretty cool.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.nitrome.com/games/finalninja/" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Final Ninja
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         9. Gunmaster Onslaught 2.0
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="gunmaster onslaught game" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/gunmasteronslaughtgame.jpg" title="gunmaster onslaught game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        On Gunmaster Onslaught, you play an army commando who has to stay alive as long as possible by surviving the assault of the enemies. At your disposal, you have guns, mines, and even rocket launchers! Move around to collect the ammo as well.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.newgrounds.com/portal/view/303877" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Gunmaster Onslaught
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         10. Robokill
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="robokill flash game" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/robokillflashgame.jpg" title="robokill flash game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Very engaging game where you play a mercenary robot trying to destroy the invaders of Titan Prime. There are several levels, each with a large number of interconnected rooms that you need to go through. You will also earn money, which allows you to buy new weapons and armor.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.rocksolidarcade.com/games/robokill/" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Robokill
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         11. N
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="n game" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/ngame.jpg" title="n game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        One of the most famous games on the web. On N, you get to play a Ninja who needs to capture golden cubes and escape the level within 90 seconds. On your way, you will find mines, lasers and even heat-seeking missiles! The physics involved and the overall game play are superb.
        <br/>
        <a href="http://www.addictinggames.com/ngame.html">
         <br/>
         Click here to play N
        </a>
       </p>
       <h2>
        Aim and Shoot Games
       </h2>
       <p>
        <strong>
         12. Throw Paper
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="throw paper game" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/throwpapergame.jpg" title="throw paper game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Very simple game where you need to throw a ball of paper on the bin. The direction arrow keeps swinging on both directions, and there is always a bit of lateral wind to increase the challenge. The objective is to hit the bin as many times in a row as possible.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.widro.com/throwpaper.html" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Throw Paper
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         13.  Bowmaster
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="bowmaster flash game" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/bowmasterflashgame.jpg" title="bowmaster flash game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Bowmaster has some strategy and RPG elements, but you will win the game with the accuracy of your aim. All you have is your bow, and you need to defend your castle from a horde of assaulting ogres. Your mouse controls both the direction and the power of the arrows.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.lostvectors.com/bowmaster/ " rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Bowmaster
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         14. Cyrkam Airtos
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="cirkam airtos game" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/cirkamairtosgame.jpg" title="cirkam airtos game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        On this game, you have to catch a paper ball that will be thrown at you by a friend, then shoot it on the bin. The shooting part is controlled by your mouse movements. Every time you score, the bin will also be moved backwards or forward.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://games.sticky.tv/cyrkam_airtos/" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Cyrkam Airtos
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         15. Bowman
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="bowman flash game" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/bowmanflashgame.jpg" title="bowman flash game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        An archery game where there is no target. Instead, you get to shoot your arrows directly at another opponent! It can be played both against the computer and against another human player (each one taking a turn).
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.bow-man.net/game.html" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Bowman
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         16. Binball Wizard
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="binball wizard game" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/binballwizardgame.jpg" title="binball wizard game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Another bin-throwing game  but this time, instead of a paper ball, you get to kick a soccer ball. The scenario is a standard office, and the bin is moved around each time you score. The physics effects definitely boost the game quality.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.binballwizard.com/" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Binball Wizard
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         17. Bloons
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="bloons flash game" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/bloonsflashgame.jpg" title="bloons flash game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Very addictive game where you play a dart-throwing monkey. On each level, you will have a large number of balloons, a specific number of dart throws, and a required number of balloons to pop.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.ninjakiwi.com/bloons.html" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Bloons
        </a>
       </p>
       <h2>
        Arcade and Classic Games
       </h2>
       <p>
        <strong>
         18. Commander Keen
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="commander keen game" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/commanderkeengame.jpg" title="commander keen game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        If you never played Commander Keen, you are with the minority. This classic has been revived on Flash, and while the quality is not outstanding, it will sure entertain the series fans for a while.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.glenrhodes.com/flashkeen/tilepop.html" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Commander Keen
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         19. Tetris
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="tetris flash" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/tetrisflash.jpg" title="tetris flash" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Perhaps the most famous game world wide, we sure could not leave it out of the list. Tetris is guaranteed to keep anyone busy for a couple of hours. The Flash version is pretty basic, but it gets the job done.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.fugly.com/flash/819/flash-tetris.html" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Tetris
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         20. Frogger
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="frogger flash" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/frogger.jpg" title="frogger" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        The game hasnt change at all since its debut on arcade machines many years ago. Get the little frog from his home to the top of the screen  all while crossing a highway full of vehicles and a river where you have to step on logs to avoid crocodiles.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.thepcmanwebsite.com/media/frogger/frogger.shtml" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Frogger
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         21. Pong
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="pong flash" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/pongflash.jpg" title="pong flash" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        The very first video game ever is also available on Flash. This little piece of game is coming straight from 1972! Just move your paddle and dont miss the ball.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.gamegum.com/game/663/pong/" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Pong
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         22. Insane Orb
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="insane orb" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/insaneorbflashgame.jpg" title="insane orb flash game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        You can also play a more hardcore version of Pong called Insane Orb. The principle is the same, but on the different levels you will have gravity fields, bouncing blocks and other items.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.2flashgames.com/f/f-579.htm" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Insane Orb
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         23. Space Invaders
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="space invaders" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/spaceinvaders.jpg" title="space invaders" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        When a game has its own Wikipedia page, you know it must be good, right? This is one of the earliest shooting games ever and also the top rated arcade game by the Guinness World Records book.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.thepcmanwebsite.com/media/flash_space_invaders/" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Space Invaders
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         24. Super Smash Flash
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="super smash flash" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/supersmashflash.jpg" title="super smash flash" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Super Smash Bros, anyone? If you never played it, it is basically a fighting game where you can match the characters from several Nintendo game titles, including Mario, Zelda and Pokemon. Not as good as the original (the game was released for the Nintendo64, after all), but still funny to play.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.newgrounds.com/portal/view/333995" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Super Smash Flash
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         25. Pacman
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="pacman game" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/09/pacmanflash.jpg" title="pacman flash" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>

        Quite a brain teaser. On Planarity you have blue dots (called vertices) connected by lines (called edges). You basically have to reorganize the vertices by dragging them around so that no two lines intersect.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.planarity.net/" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Planirity
        </a>
       </p>

         Click here to play Run Run
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         126. Orisinal Dog Game
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="orisinal dog game" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/orisinaldoggame.jpg" title="orisinal dog game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Like in Run Run, youll have to avoid the obstacles on a side-scrolling environment in Orisinal Dog. On this game, however, you control four dogs at the same time. Move them forward or backward to synchronize the jumps.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.ferryhalim.com/orisinal/g3/dog.htm" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Orisinal Dog Game
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         127. Too Many Ninjas
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="too many ninjas" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/toomanyninjas.jpg" title="too many ninjas" width="401"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Use the arrow keys to move your sword around, and block the ninjas and their throwing stars. Can you survive the assault?
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.foddy.net/Ninjas.html" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Too Many Ninjas
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         128. Sneek
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="sneek" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/sneek.jpg" title="sneek" width="394"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Keep your mouse inside the moving box for as long as possible. Careful with the distractions that will appear.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.channel4.com/entertainment/games/gameson4/gameguru/sneeek/" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Sneek
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         129. Winter Bells
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="winter bells" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/winterbellsgame.jpg" title="winter bells game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Assume the control of a cute little rabbit and jump from bell to bell. Make sure to hit the birds as well, as they will double your score. The background music is quite pleasant as well.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.ferryhalim.com/orisinal/g3/bells.htm" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Winter Bells
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         130. Nex Game
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="nex game" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/nexgame.jpg" title="nex game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Click the mouse at the right time to break the ice wall. One second too early or too late, and youll end up smashing your nose against it. Tip: When you reach the last wall, break it with a headbutt.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.gamefudge.com/Nex" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Nex Game
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         131. Flash Tron
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="flash tron" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/flashtron1.jpg" title="flash tron1" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Did you ever play Snake on a Nokia phone? This is similar, but more elaborate. You control a cycle that builds a wall after itself. You need to out maneuvre your opponent so that she will hit a wall before you do. The cycles have turbos and everything.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.fltron.com/index_flash.html" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Flash Tron
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         132. The Game of Disorientation
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="disorientation game" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/disorientationgame.jpg" title="disorientation game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Use the arrow keys to move your character around. You objective is to walk until you hit the colored square on each level. Sound easy? Heck, wait until your world starts rotating around.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://jiggmin.com/play.php?game=the_Game_of_Disorientation" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play The Game of Disorientation
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         133. The Helicopter Game
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="helicopter game" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/helicoptergame.jpg" title="helicopter game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        This little game is sure to make you waste a lot of time. Simply hold your mouse button to make the helicopter fly upward, and release it to make the helicopter go down. Reaching the first 1,000 meters is the hardest part!
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.helicoptergame.net/" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play The Helicopter Game
        </a>
       </p>
       <h2>
        Sports Games
       </h2>
       <p>
        <strong>
         134. Bumper Ball
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="bumper ball" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/bumperball.jpg" title="bumper ball" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        What happens if you mix bumper cars with soccer? Bumper Ball! Control your car with the arrow keys, and hit the ball (or your opponent) to score as many goals as possible within one minute. If no goal is scored, a Golden Goal time will follow.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://bumperball.com/" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Bumper Ball
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         135. Snowball Fight
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="snowball fight" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/snowballfight.jpg" title="snowball fight" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Choose your characters face, and wipe out everyone else in the room. Use the arrow keys to move left and right, and the mouse to throw the snow balls. They even created a jingle song for the game!
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.tapeonline.com/snowball/" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Snowball Fight
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         136. Necrathlon
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="necrathlon" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/necrathlon.jpg" title="necrathlon" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Grave hurdles. Tomb lift. Six foot dig. Skull put. The Necrathlon! Hilarious game concept. You need to compete on those four different modalities to obtain a final score. Careful to not destroy your keyboard
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.gamesforwork.com/games/play-4626-Necrathalon-Flash_Game" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Necrathlon
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         137. Penguin Dive
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="penguin dive" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/penguindiveflashgame.jpg" title="penguin dive flash game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Press space to start the motion, space again to jump (try to do this before the flag), and then use the arrow keys to add rotation to your jump and to calculate the entrance. There are three criteria for the points: height, rotation and dive entry.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.adobe.com/macromedia/holiday2004/" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Penguin Dive
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         138. Dolphin Olympics 2
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="dolphin olympics 2" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/dolphinolympics.jpg" title="dolphin olympics" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Score as many points as possible in two minutes by swimming and flipping your dolphin. Successful jumps build speed, allowing for bigger and better tricks. Use all the arrow keys to rotate and spin the dolphin.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.kongregate.com/games/arawkins/dolphin-olympics-2" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Dolphin Olympics 2
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         139. Max Dirt Bike
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="max dirt bike" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/maxdirtbikegame.jpg" title="max dirt bike game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Terrific game where you need to pass several obstacles with your motorcycle (ever see trials competitions on television?). Use the up and down arrows to accelerate and brake, and the left and right arrows to balance the motorcycle.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.addictinggames.com/maxdirtbike.html" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Max Dirt Bike
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         140. Tennis Game
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="tennis game" class="bord" height="200" src="http://www.techcult.com/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/tennisgame.jpg" title="tennis game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        The classic tennis game (remember the one for NES?). Use the arrow keys to move and space to hit the ball. The arrows control the direction of the hit as well. You can play either an exhibition match or the world championship.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.play.vg/games/142-Tennis%20Game.html">
         <br/>
         Click here to play Tennis Game
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         141. Yeti Sports
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="yeti sports" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/yetisports.jpg" title="yeti sports" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        There are 14 mini games inside this portal. It requires registration, but it is worth it. Albatroz Overload? Penguin Baseball? They have it all!
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.yetisports.org/en/online.php" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Yeti Sports
        </a>
       </p>
       <h2>
        Strategy Games
       </h2>
       <p>
        <strong>
         142. Invasion Tactical Defense
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="invasion tactical defense" class="bord" height="200" src="http://www.techcult.com/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/invasiontacticaldefense.jpg" title="invasion tactical defense" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Aliens are invading Earth, and you have to defend an important nuclear factory. Do this by buying cannons and tell them what to do. You also have to make strategic decisions about what cannons you buy and what upgrades you make.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.newgrounds.com/portal/view/393072" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Invasion Tactical Defense
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         143. Lemonade Stand
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="lemonade stand" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/lemmonadestand.jpg" title="lemonade stand" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        You have 30 days to run your lemonade stand. How much money can you make? Every day, you need to decide how much to spend on advertising, how much to charge for each glass, and how many glasses to produce. Tip: Check the weather on the window.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.insanecentral.com/arcade/game/22/Lemonade-stand.html" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Lemonade Stand
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         144. Star Dominion
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="star dominion" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/stardominion.jpg" title="star dominion" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Probably the best real-time Flash strategy game out there. Mine resources and build towns, defense systems, research new technologies and train units in order to attack the enemy bases and capture resources controlled by the enemy.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.gamenode.com/online/games/star-dominion/" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Star Dominion
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         145. Sea of Fire
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="sea of fire" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/seaoffire.jpg" title="sea of fire" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Construct buildings on the empty tiles, and make them produce units. The units will automatically attack the enemy base and soldiers. The objective is to destroy all the enemy structures. Money is earned as time elapses, but you can increase the interest rates with special financial buildings. Engaging game.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://fpflashfarm.com/FB49PFBFFKJ42BF/13888_seaoffire.swf" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Sea of Fire
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         146. Dice Wars
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="dice wars" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/dicewar.jpg" title="dice wars" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Turn-based strategy game where you have to conquer the territories of your opponents by attacking them with your dice. (The sum of the numbers of the attacking dice must be bigger than that of the defending dice.) At the end of each turn, you will receive as many dice as the number of adjacent territories that you control.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.gamedesign.jp/flash/dice/dice.html" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Dice Wars
        </a>
       </p>
       <h2>
        Weird Games
       </h2>
       <p>
        <strong>
         147. The Last Guy
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="the last guy" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/lastguygame.jpg" title="last guy game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Japanese coders are really creative. This game allows you to turn any Web site into an online game! You control a little bug, and your objective is to rescue the other bugs around the field.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://lastguy.jp/" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play The Last Guy
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         148. Flow
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="flow flash game" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/flowflashgame.jpg" title="flow flash game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Created for a thesis project, this game is really revolutionary. You simply swim around with your multi-cellular organism. Eat other organisms to grow and evolve. Creatures with a red dot will take you to a deeper level (20 total). Pay attention to the integration between the intro, the game play and the credits. Simply beautiful.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://intihuatani.usc.edu/cloud/flowing/" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Flow
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         149. Jelly Jumper
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="jelly jumper" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/jellyjumper.jpg" title="jelly jumper" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Use the arrow keys to guide the chubby little guy around. There are 50 levels to go, and you will need to step on the right keys. The game was sponsored by Logitech.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www.gamenet.com/game/jellyjumper/" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Jelly Jumper
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         150. Kill The Popups
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="kill the popups flash game" class="bord" height="200" src="/wp-content/uploads/2008/10/killthepopupsgame.jpg" title="kill the popups game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        If you have been using the Internet for a while, you probably already have a good training for this game. Kill the popups before the take control of the screen. Crazy adaptation of
        <i>
         The Ride of The Valkyries
        </i>
        song as well  check it out.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://www2.b3ta.com/realistic-internet-simulator/" rel="nofollow">
         Click here to play Kill The Popups
        </a>

       <br/>
       <p>
        Funky background music and a gameplay that makes you remember Worms. On this multiplayer game players will need to fire projectiles against each other, and the action is divided in turns. On each round you will have two teams with three players each. Pretty cool.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://zwok-game.com/en_IE/" rel="nofollow">

        Use your mouse to point and shoot, and the WASD keys to move, duck and jump. Kill all the enemies on the other side of street. The game has some slick graphics, check it out.

       </p>
       <p>

       <center>
        <img alt="coign of vintage" class="bord" height="200" src="http://www.techcult.com/wp-content/uploads/2008/11/coign-of-vintage.jpg" title="coign of vintage" width="400"/>

        <strong>
         154. Puzzle Farter
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <center>
        <img alt="puzzlefarter flash game" class="bord" height="200" src="http://www.techcult.com/wp-content/uploads/2008/11/puzzlefarter-flash-game.jpg" title="puzzlefarter flash game" width="400"/>
       </center>
       <br/>
       <p>
        Can you fart with precision? Well, you can test that with this game! Use the arrow keys to control a little guy that can fly around using his farts! There are 50 levels to go, and on each you need to reach the exit door while avoiding the obstacles. The sounds are hilarious.
       </p>
       <p>
        <a href="http://puzzlefarter.com/" rel="nofollow">

         <p>
          You dont have any of Mateusz Skutniks games!
         </p>
         <p>
          If you want games that are difficult, well drawn, have great plots, and are sometimes creepy or even scary, you need to play his games.  You can find them all at
          <a href="http://www.pastelstories.com/" rel="nofollow">
           pastelstories.com
          </a>
          !
         </p>
         <p>
          Play the Submachine series, a legendary series of point and click adventures. You have to collect items, solve puzzles, and even travel through time and space to escape oppressive enviornments.  There are several of these available, and should keep you busy for a long time!  Go to
          <a href="http://www.pastelportal.com/stories/the-submachines/" rel="nofollow">
           the Submachines
          </a>
          .
         </p>
         <p>
          Theres also the creepy Day Mare Town series.  You find yourself trapped in a creepy, nearly deserted town with seemingly no way out.  Interact with ominous characters, collect items and solve eerie, challenging puzzles to escape.  The link is
          <a href="http://www.daymaretown.com/" rel="nofollow">
           Daymare Town
          </a>
          .
         </p>
         <p>
          Then try the epic Covert Front series, where you play as undercover agent Kara in an alternative realitys version of World War 1.  Collect items, solve puzzles and explore eerie environments as you investigate the abduction and disappearance of general Karl von Toten.  The link is
          <a href="http://www.pastelportal.com/stories/covert-front/" rel="nofollow">
           Covert Front
          </a>
          .
         </p>
         <p>
          Good luck, and enjoy!
         </p>

          To download these games using your download manager just add swf as the extension to download while clicking on the links provided to the flash games. But remove the swf extension after your download has been complete otherwise unnecessarily unwanted flash ones will be downloaded. download only the ones which have sizes greater than 1mb(can vary in ranges of few 100kbs also) and neglect flash below 30-40kb.
